**Spacing Layout:**

- Corporate presentation templates include guidelines for layout, spacing, and alignment.

**Brand Voice:**

- Overview and examples of Adobe's editorial voice, reflecting brand personality and differentiation in written communication.

**Notes:**

- General guidelines on Adobe brand assets use, legal notices, and email submission for review. Additional resources for brand assistance and related materials.
